< text>
The title is a bit confusing since it's Korean fried chicken and not barbecue, but for what it's worth, this place is the best. The chicken is crisp and all the flavor is on point. As others have said the wait is a bit long, but everything is made to order, so I'd say it's worth it.

Also note worthy is their specials, they have good specials with their "friends" combo and such which offer chicken a side dish and a pitcher of beer. If you're in for lunch they have a nice simple lunch special which is 2 drum sticks and 2 sides.</text>

Typical Korean chicken place where you wait at least 15-20 min to get your delicious fried chicken
We ordered half original and half sweet and spicy.
Original was delicious..hot and crunchy on the outside and tender/hot on the inside. The sweet and spicy chicken was not so great..it was more sweet and not spicy at all. will not order this again next time.
Mac and cheese looked good, but once it enters your moth, you realize how watered down it is.
Onion rings as great! Crispy and hot and did not fall apart after you bit into it. Honey mustard sauce with onion rings was perfect!
Korean rice cake was hot and cooked to chewy perfection but was not spicy.
Customer service was good.
Good for late night dinner or snack< /review>

<review>So I realized my last visit here was in 2008. And if a place has been around that long, it should've improved right?

The service was definitely better and they also have lunch specials now (even on weekends)

But we opted for the $20 Half and Half which was 5 pieces Olive Chicken and 9 pieces of Sweet/Spicy. I would've preferred it, if the 9 pieces were olive chicken though as the sweet/spicy gets overpowering.

The olive chicken was really good though, and had a super light batter.

It came with a bowl of radish cubes (love) and a plate of cabbage drizzled with thousand island.

Maybe it's just me, but regardless of olive oil preparation, anytime I want fried chicken, I'll still automatically think of Popeyes first. xD

But this place is good for KOREAN fried chicken with the super crispy light batter. Try the lunch specials first ;)<//review><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< Response>

< Review>
****Update****

Ok, I have had it with this place. I have defended their bad service, but no more. It is so bad that I don't care how good it tastes, its now a bad experience. And I think the chickens are getting smaller. Barely any meat on the birds! No ice in drinks, no service for refills, no more cabbage salad, loud and noisy, dirty, disorganized. I asked for tabasco sauce and they said they are out.

Previous review:

I have a love hate relationship with this place. I love it because the olive oil whole plain chicken is so good. I have tried so many places and this place has the best tasting chicken. The batter is flakey and crispy. Chicken is moist, Its a unique coating on this chicken. I love the free pickles and the free cabbage salad you get as well.

Why they call it BBQ chicken is beyond me. It should be called Fried Chicken?

But the service is so sub par. They always forget to bring out the free radish pickles and cabbage. I always have to ask. Why??!! It's such a simple process. I seriously have had to ask the last 5 times we have eaten here. It's not like it's a complicated menu for the people to learn and remember!

I also hate how they are so stingy on ice in the drinks. Props for giving you huge cups for soft drinks, but always so little ice. And they will refill your drinks without an issue, but more often than not, they wont refill ice unless you ask.

I want to give this place more stars so they stay in business because I love the chicken. All they need to do is provide better customer service. This place changes owners often. They just repainted the inside. I don't know why they keep spending the money on things that don't matter (repainting the decorations on the inside) vs providing better customer service.

Stop having such young kids work the store. Time for some adults to provide customer service!

I hate you BBQ Chicken, I love you BBQ Chicken, I hate you BBQ Chicken</Review>

<Name>Jason Lum< /Name><time>1458230093112< /time><rate>3<//rate><review>BBQ Chicken is Korean food? What? The name always throws me off. Especially, if you are looking for some Southern Food. This is a different kind of Seoul Food.

I was a bit skeptical at first, because the idea of Olive fried chicken is about as appealing as a Diet Coke. I always cook with Olive oil, but I hate to break it to you (health nuts) but deep frying in Olive Oil is the same as any oil. If you use gallons of oil, there's no health benefit over vegetable or canola. Also, vegetable oil has a high smoking point making it ideal for frying, but Olive oil will taste like burnt candles if heated over a certain temperature. I promise I will not bore you with anymore food science. If you are trying to stay health by eating Olive Oil fried chicken, go somewhere else and peel the skin off or dab your pizza, because this place like a diet soda IS NOT HEALTHIER. Also, be prepared to pay a butt-load for Fried Chicken which is normally a relatively cheap food.

To be honest with you the food at BBQ Chicken real isn't that bad. Every time I go the restaurant is packed and has a decent atmosphere. I never really had much trouble with service. The servers try to be extra friendly, but I have heard complaints about servers that don't give much service to women. That's understandable haha jk. Sometimes women tend to get jealous of other women...

However, for the price and the value. The chicken Meh! A whole chicken cost about 20 dollars roughly after tax for about 8 pieces. It is not finger licking good. I hate to copy another review..but go to KFC instead. Personally, after eating I felt like driving the 15 or 20 miles to go Popeye's instead. $20 probably would get a nice 20 piece bucket of spicy Louisiana style friend chicken.

If money is not an issue and you are looking for Korean food with a twist, give it a try. If you are looking for Fried Chicken, go elsewhere. Sometimes Korean Mixes are good like Amerie, very hot! However, BBQ Chicken is not recommend for hardcore Fried Chicken lovers.</review><Pics>None<//Pics><Response>None< /Response><gmap_id>0x80dcde9d7036af77:0xcf173dd87df8d562< /gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

<Rate>1</Rate>< Text>
Awful, winery absolutely never going there again. My friend (former tasting manager) highly recommended it so we went. Apparently this winery is hurting for money as their tasting room manager and staff keep track of every wine glass they give with each tasting and charge you it if it's not returned after you leave the winery. You get no warning nor does it say anywhere if you take the glass that they will charge you for it so you don't know they do it unless you check your transactions. A wedding party was having their rehearsal was finishing up while we were there and once they left one of the staff complained to the tasting manager that they took 6 glasses and his response was "don't worry we'll charge the bride for them." Mind you this couple is spending thousands of dollars at their winery and they're going to charge the bride unknownly for all those glasses. Not cool and distasteful on their part and wonder if that's even legal to charge you after you leave especially when they no longer have your credit card? The tasting manager (the only one pouring) also took a long phone call while we were there which was rude and he completely forgot about us once another couple came in that was a lot younger (there were only 4 customers total doing the tasting). My girlfriend felt bad and embarrassed for bringing me there as this was the worst experience we've ever had at a winery.<//Text>

<Date>1520713764216</Date>< review>
The car wash is as good as most automatic washes and thankfully they reclaim their water. Additionally, if you buy the highest level wash they will re wash it within 72 hours at no cost. The one piece of their business that rubbed me wrong was that they advertise that if it rains within 72 hours of your wash they will also re wash it. The problem is that you have to have it re washed within the 72 hours even if it is still raining. To me this means their push to have you get it washed even if it might rain soon is very misleading and now I know not to trust that.<//review>

< review>
The price of the carwash isn't too bad $6.95 I paid. But the car wash itself was fairly poor. It didn't do the rims very well and the people who sprayed the pre-wash on didn't really get the whole car so as a result it wasn't very clean when I came out and the air dryer didn't dry the car off very well. On the plus side, the vacume area was nice. Hoses on both sides of your car. Nice long hose length. Detail attachments on the ends. Floormat clip boards for hanging your floormats. Trash cans on both sides. And untimed self vacume ability was included in the price of the carwash. The place was tidy. Garbage cans kept emptied. I found it a bit cramped to drive around at in a larger vehicle but managable.
Its certianly much nicer looking with its modern glass walls letting you view the cars go thru the wash and better equipped vacume wise than the self serve carwash down the block. But if you dont mind doing it yourself and like a little elbow room and a wash that gets off the heavy grime and dont need the entertainment of seeing how a drivethru carwash works then skip going to Splash. It's basicly only good for a quicky exterior wash job and a really good vacume.
But for the price just the untimed vacume is worth going there thats why i gave it a 3 star rating.</review>
